<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stichten.html>stichten</a> (8123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stichten.html>stichten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiften.html>stiften</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stihten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stiftijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stichten.html>stichten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to found, establish</li>
<li>to cause, allow to occur</li>
<li>to preach</li></ol>

***stiekum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stiekum.html>stiekum</a> (72697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekem.html>stiekem</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekum.html>stiekum</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> north-western Germany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> discreetly, secretly
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mach.html>mach</a> ich <a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekum.html>stiekum</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> kriegt keiner mit.</i>
<dl><dd>I do that quite <b>discreetly</b>. Nobody will know.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common chiefly in the western <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of Westphalia. In adjacent regions it also widely understood, but not often <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a>.
</p>
</body> 
***stiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stiel.html>stiel</a> (62870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiel.html>stiel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estile</i>. Doublet with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a></i>.

***stig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stig.html>stig</a> (29616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stīgō</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stīganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">climb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ( gt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stīgan</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stige</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stiga</i>. A masculine Germanic variant <i>*stīgaz</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indicated by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stic</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:steig.html>Steig</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">stígr</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:stig.html>stig</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">stīġ</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">stīġa</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">stīġe</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>path (especially steep or narrow)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stiją</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">stí</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sti</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">stiġ</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang"><strong class="selflink">stiġ</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hall, building, sty</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stigen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stīgan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stīganą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijgen.html>stijgen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to climb, to go up, to rise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ascend</li></ol>

***stijl.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a> (2384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stilus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijlen.html>stijlen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>style, fashion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> style of a pistil</li>
<li>a <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> on a metal fence</li>
<li>the vertical part of the metal or concrete support frame that surrounds a window or a <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stille.html>stille</a> (5283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stille.html>stille</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stillen.html>stillen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>silent person, who rarely speaks</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:undercover.html>undercover</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> (male only)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stille.html>stille</a></strong>
</p>

<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***stilleven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleven</a> (50623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stil.html>stil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still, motionless, silent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps from older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilstaand.html>stilstaand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleven</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stillevens.html>stillevens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleventje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">still-life</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">painting or other image of arranged inanimate or dead <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, sometimes displaying living animals as well</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from late 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1678</b>, Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Hoogstraeten, <i>Inleyding <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Hooge Schoole <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Schilderkonst: <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>Anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Zichtbaere Werelt</i>, publ. by Fransois <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Hoogstraeten, page 87.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echter.html>Echter</a> ſtaet <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> vaſt, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> overaerdig eenige <a href = vnd.unilang:bloemen.html>bloemen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vruchten.html>vruchten</a>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <b>ſtillevens</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> wy'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a>, geſchildert <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, deeze Schilderyen <a href = vnd.unilang:evenwel.html>evenwel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> hooger, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> in den eerſten graed <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> konſtwerken moogen geſtelt <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> waerenze <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Heem</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>Pater</a> Zegers</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jae.html>jae</a> Zeuxis <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Parraſius, <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> bedriegens <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> uitgevoert.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">However, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> certain, that no matter how exceedingly charming some flowers, fruits or other <b>still <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a></b>, as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> call it, have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> painted, these paintings may nevertheless not be placed any <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> than in the first [lowest] degree of artworks; <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> if they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> executed to the point of deceptive realism by <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Heem, father Zegers, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> Zeuxis and Parrhasius.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***stinky.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a> (25162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">stynky</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stink.html>stink</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stinkig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a>, foul, <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stinkig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hunsrik" class="extiw" title="w:Hunsrik">Hunsrik</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hrx">stinkich</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">stinkier</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">stinkiest</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Having a strong, unpleasant smell; stinking.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Bad, undesirable.
<ul><li><b>1991,</b> Theresa P. Gladden, <i>Romancing Susan</i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=e-NgFsYD8vEC">[1]</a></sup> Bantam Books, →ISBN, page 37,
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> she walked <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to the table and switched off the <a href = vnd.unilang:walkman.html>Walkman</a> as she <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> down.</dd>
<dd>“Hey!” <a href = vnd.unilang:nikki.html>Nikki</a> yelped. “That <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b> thing to do. That <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> my favorite song.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2003,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:betty.html>Betty</a> Levin, <i>Shoddy Cove</i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=KsSG2j82PJAC">[2]</a></sup> HarperCollins, →ISBN, page 151,
<dl><dd>“School all year round.” The father groaned. “What a good idea.”</dd>
<dd>“Stupid, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b> idea,” a child remarked from across the room.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007,</b> Aletha V. Smithson, “Pacifier Breaking” (poem), in <i>As He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> Known</i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=8BzMlduE8R8C">[3]</a></sup> AuthorHouse, →ISBN, page 172,
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:binky.html>binky</a> drifted up and far away,</dd>
<dd>To the <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> in the moon, I <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> them say;</dd>
<dd>A cute idea but a <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b> plan.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***stoel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a> (1335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stuol</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stōlaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoelen.html>stoelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoeltje.html>stoeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chair, sitting furniture, normally mobile and on four <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></li>
<li>(hence) Any seat, from stool to throne; a dais
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetel.html>zetel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>The base, e.g. platform, on which something rests; something fixed on it, notably a workbench</li>
<li>A place of residence, headquarters, powerbase</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> receptacle, stool, a type of stump</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> confessional chair
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:biechtstoel.html>biechtstoel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fecal stool
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoelgang.html>stoelgang</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> toadstool
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddenstoel.html>paddenstoel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***stoer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoer.html>stoer</a> (4346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally the same word as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurs</a></i>, of which it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an eastern dialectal variant. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stur</i> (itself from Low German). Not immediately cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stour</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">stor</i>, but possibly related.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>firm, robust, sturdy<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li>tough, <a href = vnd.unilang:cool.html>cool</a></li></ol>

***stoet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoet.html>stoet</a> (24735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoet.html>stoet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stuot</i> (attested as <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stōti</i>), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stuot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stōdą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***stof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a> (2062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stubą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stofje.html>stofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dust</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoffen.html>stoffe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estophe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estoffe</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estoffer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stoffōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stuppōn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cram, plug, stuff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stoff</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stuff</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoffen.html>stoffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stofje.html>stofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>matter, material</li>
<li>substance</li>
<li>fabric</li>
<li>curriculum</li></ol>
